1935.08.04

Various Hubei Government Conferences Decide on Flood Control Plans; Dredging the Yangtze River to be Overseen by the Water Conservancy Association; Dredging the Xiang River to be Designed by the Engineering Bureau; River Waters Continue to Recede, Wuhan Dyke Out of Danger 1

(Hankou) Various government agencies held two meetings yesterday and today to discuss river dredging and dyke construction, deciding on five measures. Dredging of the Yangtze River will be overseen by the Water Conservancy Association; dredging of the Xiang River will be designed by the Jianghan Engineering Bureau; investigations into dykes and embankments, as well as repairs, relief for refugees through work, and conscription of labor, will all have implementation measures determined. It is reported that the Jianghan Bureau has received orders to repair breached dykes and has scheduled construction to begin before the 15th, and has requested 2 million [dollars] to repair the Wuhan dykes. (3rd Day Special Dispatch)

(Hankou) The river water receded to 45.8 on the 3rd, a total drop of 5.7 feet. The Wuhan Dyke is out of danger and has been taken over by the Jianghan Bureau. Due to the slow receding of water in various counties, it will be difficult to replant autumn crops. Cheng Qibao and Li Shucheng telegraphed Zhang Qun separately, stating that it would be best to allocate relief funds quickly. The Wuhan Expanded Fundraising Committee is scheduled to hold a meeting in Hankou on the 4th. (3rd Day Special Dispatch)

(Hankou) The Hubei Construction Department, upon the order of the Provincial Government, convened the Civil Affairs Department, the Jianghan Engineering Bureau, the Flood Relief Association, and other agencies on the 2nd and 3rd to discuss the two issues of dredging rivers and repairing dykes and dams, in order to submit a report to Chairman Chiang for review and instructions. Three principles were decided: (1) Dredging of the Yangtze River will be handled comprehensively by the Water Conservancy Commission. (2) Dredging of the silted Xiang River will be undertaken by the Jianghan Engineering Bureau and the Construction Department in consultation to formulate a concrete action plan. (3) Breached dykes will be repaired with work-for-relief programs, and detailed plans will be made after the relief funds arrive. (3rd Day Central News Agency Dispatch)

Gucheng Suffers Another Flood Disaster 2

(Hankou) According to a telegram from Xiangyang, Zhang Qun reported that Gucheng suffered another flood disaster. On the morning of the 1st, the Nan River rose by more than 1 zhang (approx. 10 feet) within one hour. Replanted autumn crops in areas where the water had receded on both banks were almost completely submerged. The floodwaters once again reached the city walls, threatening to enter the city. The county magistrate and garrison troops are blocking the city gates, collecting civilian boats in preparation for flood prevention and rescue. (3rd Day Special Dispatch)

Hutuo River Surges; Raoyang Embankment Breached 3

(Tianjin) The Hutuo River in the middle reaches surged by six feet. A section of the embankment in Raoyang County, which had not been repaired for many years, finally breached on the 2nd, causing widespread flooding. More than 40 villages, including Liuge Dian and Genggezhuang, have become a watery expanse. The rushing torrents have also flooded more than 20 villages in the neighboring Xian County, causing severe disaster. Within Quzhou territory, the Fu River is overflowing and continuing to rise, creating a dangerous situation. Several thousand residents in more than a hundred villages on both banks are desperately working day and night to reinforce the embankments. (3rd Day Special Dispatch)

(Tianjin) On the 3rd, the water level at the Yongding River's Zhegou Bridge and Huilong Temple was 60.89 meters, an increase of 1.2 centimeters from the previous day. The water level in the middle reaches of Qujiadian on the 3rd was 50.94 meters, and the flow rate remained rapid. (3rd Day Special Dispatch)

Fengpei County Magistrate Supervises Emergency Dyke Reinforcement 4

(Xuzhou) The Special Commissioner's Office received a telegram from Pei County stating that the breach in Yutai had caused water to flow to Gaozhuang, putting the new dyke in a critical state. Shao Hanyuan went to Pei County this morning to supervise and coordinate with the Pei County Magistrate in leading the laborers to reinforce the dyke. A telegram from Feng County stated that the eastern branch of the Yi River in the second district of northern Feng County was facing a backflow from the lake, threatening to breach. Feng County Magistrate Wang Shuxian rushed to the dyke to supervise the inspection and reinforcement of the river dyke. The northern parts of Feng and Pei counties remain in a critical situation. (3rd Day Special Dispatch)

(Xuzhou) The Hanzhuang Water Station reported that the water level at the lake outlet is currently 32.145 meters, and the water level in the Grand Canal is 32.077 meters. (3rd Day Special Dispatch)

(Xuzhou) Yu Shufang went to Gaozhuang, north of Pei County, yesterday to survey the flood situation and returned to Xuzhou in the evening. According to him, the speed of the water entering Fengpei after the breach is still slow. It is said that the water level has dropped in western Shandong after the dyke breach caused flooding, indicating that there is no large flow coming from upstream. Fengpei may be able to avoid danger, but without plugging the breach at Linpu Settlement, there is no certainty for northern Jiangsu. Yu is going to Nanjing tonight to attend the Economic Commission meeting and will return to Xuzhou after the meeting. The Shandong Construction Department dispatched engineer Liu Mengjiu to Xuzhou on the 3rd to inspect the Shuangzha and Linjiaba at the lake outlet to understand the impact of the slightly lower water washing downstream. He is scheduled to go to Pei County on the 4th to inspect the new dyke before going to Beijing to attend the Economic Commission meeting. (3rd Day Special Dispatch)

Water Level of Weishan Lake Reaches Level with Embankment 5

(Jinan) Zhang Honglie, accompanied by Wang Shaochang, took a boat from Jining along the Grand Canal to Nanyang Lake today to inspect the situation. The water situation was very serious. They returned to Jining in the evening and transferred to Yanzhou. They are scheduled to go to Beijing on the 4th to attend the Economic Commission meeting on behalf of Han Fuqu. The water level of Weishan Lake has reached the level of the embankment. If there is a strong wind, it will overflow immediately, and the water will inevitably return to the old course of the Yellow River. Jinxiang and Yutai counties are currently rushing to reinforce the embankment. (3rd Day Special Dispatch)

Hurricane Approaches Xiamen Again; Customs Raises Warning Flag 6

(Xiamen) The sky cleared on the 3rd. At 6:00 PM, the customs received a report that a hurricane had formed at 2:30 PM at 124 degrees east longitude and 23 degrees north latitude. It is more severe than the previous two and is 60 nautical miles from Xiamen. The wind direction is east-northeast. It is expected to pass Xiamen at night and the customs immediately raised the warning flag. It was raining by 8:00 or 9:00 PM. (3rd Day Special Dispatch)

(Nanjing) The Central Meteorological Observatory reported that the typhoon recently discovered in the ocean northeast of the Philippine Islands reached the northeast of Taiwan at 3:00 PM, located between 123 degrees east longitude and 25 degrees north latitude, moving northwest. The wind force is very strong and will land in the Wenzhou and Fuzhou areas within 24 hours. The southeastern coast and the lower reaches of the Yangtze River are already affected, with strong winds and rain. The rainstorm in Nanjing in the afternoon of the 3rd was due to its influence. There will be continued showers on the 4th. (3rd Day Central News Agency Dispatch)

(Nanjing) There was heavy rain in Nanjing on the 3rd, and the temperature dropped to 77 degrees [Fahrenheit]. (3rd Day Special Dispatch)

(Xiamen) The rain stopped at 10:00 PM on the 3rd, and the wind had not arrived by 12:00 AM. (3rd Day Special Dispatch)

Water Recedes from Quanzhou and Zhangzhou Cities 7

(Xiamen) In the Quanzhou flood disaster, it is known that over a hundred people have died or been injured, and tens of thousands of people have been affected. Several thousand are homeless, and the estimated losses are around 3 million [dollars]. Most of the water in the city receded on the 2nd, but the suburbs are still flooded. Traffic between Quanzhou and Anxi is open to a point three miles from the city. Travel to Dongshan requires small boats. Various circles in Jinjiang have formed a disaster relief association. The water in Zhangzhou city receded very quickly on the 2nd and will be completely gone by the 3rd. The Jiulong River rose more than two zhang (approx. 20 feet) this time, and the losses are greater than before. Due to traffic disruptions in the countryside, the water situation is unknown. Traffic between Zhangzhou and Xiamen remained cut off on the 3rd. (3rd Day Special Dispatch)

(Xiamen) The flood disaster in Nan'an, Quanzhou, is also severe, and the affected area is even wider. Over a hundred li (approx. 33 miles) of farmland, villages, and towns in the Honglai wharf and Yunwei Xiwei area were submerged. Numerous corpses are flowing down the east and west streams. Several dozen bodies have been recovered outside Quanzhou city. (3rd Day Special Dispatch)

Tianjin City Dikes Repaired; Water Level of Rivers Falling 8

(Tianjin) The earth embankments on all the city's river dikes have been completed. The 28 damaged sections of the enclosure dikes were all repaired and blocked by the 3rd. The city river water level dropped one inch on the 3rd, and the flow is slowing down. (3rd Day Special Dispatch)

Han Fuqu Appeals to Kong Xiangxi to Quickly Allocate Relief Funds for Shandong Disaster 9

(Jinan) Han Fuqu telegraphed Kong Xiangxi today, stating that 5 million disaster victims have no way to appeal and are weeping and pleading, requesting that passports be issued so that they can seek food elsewhere, mostly with Nanjing as their destination. Although they have been persuaded with tactful words, they are willing to take risks. It is hoped that a large sum of money will be quickly raised to save the dying and support the living, so that aiding Shandong is the same as securing Beijing, and relieving the disaster is the same as governing the interior. He also telegraphed Xu Shiying, stating that the losses in the disaster area reached 105 million yuan. He also telegraphed Lin, Jiang, and Wang, requesting that the Ministry of Railways be ordered to repair a light railway from Lanfeng to the breach point, and that the Tianjin-Pukou and Jiaoji Railways be ordered to allocate two special trains to transport materials for plugging the breach. The China International Famine Relief Commission plans to go to the disaster area to distribute 100,000 yuan in relief. The Provincial Executive Committee telegraphed overseas Chinese compatriots, urging them to donate to disaster relief. The Hong Kong Daozi Society dispatched Ms. Huang Hengjie and three others to Jinan to purchase 4,000 bags of flour for relief. (3rd Day Special Dispatch)

Bandits Lurking and Raiding the Eastern Suburbs of Beiping 10

(Beiping) A large number of bandits have recently been lurking in the Dongbazhen area in the eastern suburbs of Beiping, constantly raiding travelers and residents, and their momentum is very rampant. The gentry and elders of the town have specially come to Beiping to submit a petition to the Beiping-Tianjin Garrison Headquarters and the Public Security Bureau, requesting that troops and police be dispatched to garrison the town. This has been approved. At present, shops and households in the town close their gates tightly at 7:00 PM every night, and soldiers and police patrol at any time. However, in the areas near the town outside of it, due to the lack of troops and police to suppress them, the bandit forces are still rampant, and residents with slightly more wealth are moving their whole families into the town to avoid the bandits. (3rd Day Special Dispatch)

Bandits Attempt to Disrupt the War Zone; Japanese Side Declares Non-Involvement 11

(Tianjin) It has been proven that the bandits disturbing the Xifengkou and Qian'an areas are remnants of Liu Guitang's troops, commanded by Bai Jianwu and Lin Yulin. They plan to sneak through various passes, claim to have 4,000 men, and carry the flags of the puppet North China Autonomous National Salvation Army in an attempt to disrupt the war zone, also claiming to have obtained the consent of the Japanese side. The Kawakishi Brigade Commander in Gubeikou dispatched staff officer Harada to declare to Huo Shisheng, the Director of the Gubeikou-Jimi Special Commissioner's Office, that the Kwantung Army Headquarters and the North China Garrison Army Headquarters had not been involved in this matter. If the name of the Japanese army is used, or the name cards of officers are used for disruptive activities, or if Japanese rōnin (masterless samurai) participate, China is allowed to take decisive measures to thoroughly resolve the matter. (3rd Day Special Dispatch)

(Tianjin) Zhang Yantian, the commander of the 2nd Security Brigade, passed through Tianjin to Beiping on the night of the 2nd to request instructions from the Military Branch on the method of suppressing bandits in Taipingzhai and Luotun in Qian'an. He left Beiping on the evening of the 3rd and rushed back to the defense area, immediately leading all his troops in a large-scale attack. (3rd Day Special Dispatch)

(Beiping) It has recently been confirmed that the bandits entrenched in the Luanyu-Jimi area and along the various passes of the Great Wall are a joint force of Bai Jianwu, Liu Guitang, and Lin Yuchun, totaling 2,200 to 2,300 men, calling themselves the Autonomous National Salvation Army. Their uniforms, weapons, and guns are complete. The Hebei Provincial Government and the leaders of the 1st and 2nd Special Police Detachments of the Luanyu-Jimi area and the Great Wall passes, Zhang Yantian and Zhang Qingyu, etc., are leading their troops and coordinating with the local militias of various counties to implement an encirclement in order to eliminate the source of the chaos. (3rd Day Special Dispatch)

Numerous Bandits Near Yuguan; Gunfire Incessant in the Suburbs 12

(Tianjin) Three hundred well-equipped bandits have been discovered near the Xishi River, west of Yuguan. Zhang Yantian, the commander of the 2nd Security Brigade, telephoned Su Yuqi on the 2nd to discuss joint suppression. Gunfire has been incessant every night in the suburbs of Yuguan, and several miles outside the city are full of bandit hideouts. (3rd Day Special Dispatch)

(Beiping) A large number of bandits, more than 300, have recently been discovered near the Xishi River area west of Yuguan, and they are well-equipped with firearms. Gunfire has been heard almost constantly every night for the past three days near the west gate of Yuguan. Zhang Yantian, the commander of the 2nd Special Police Corps of the war zone, has telephoned Su Yuqi, the director of the Yuguan Special Public Security Bureau, to go to Liushouying to discuss methods of suppressing the bandits and will jointly launch an attack. (3rd Day Special Dispatch)

Liu's Troops Flee Back to Yanqing; Occupy Hei Hanling 13

(Tianjin) More than 800 remnants of Liu Guitang's troops entrenched in the 2nd and 5th districts of Yanqing. On the 31st, they were besieged by the Yanqing County Magistrate leading local militias and police teams. After fighting for a day and a night, the bandits dispersed and fled in several directions. Unexpectedly, the county magistrate was ordered to be replaced on the 1st, and the teams were demobilized. The bandits took advantage of the situation to flee back and occupy the Hei Hanling area, and their momentum is extremely rampant. There is still a tendency to sneak into the Hebei border area across the Great Wall line. (3rd Day Special Dispatch)

Yin Rugeng Arrives in Tangshan; Formally Assumes Office 14

(Beiping) Yin Rugeng left Beiping for Tangshan this morning. At 2:00 PM this afternoon, he went to the Commissioner's Office to formally assume office. The former commissioner, Tao Shangming, will come to Beiping from Tangshan tonight or tomorrow morning to meet Wang Kemin and report on the handover process and take office as a councillor of the Political Affairs Council after the handover is completed. (3rd Day Special Dispatch)

(Tianjin) Yin Rugeng passed through Tianjin to Tangshan on the morning of the 3rd. According to him, he will arrive in Tangshan today and see how the situation allows for. If time and circumstances permit, he will assume office immediately. Otherwise, he will take over in the early morning of the 4th. The bandit atmosphere in the Ao-Yu area is indeed fierce, and the incident of a bandit group attacking and disturbing various cities and towns in Qian'an is also very serious. After assuming office, he will immediately consult with the commanders of the various security corps on methods of suppressing the bandits. As to whether Su Yuqi has agreed to take office as the Administrative Commissioner of the Jimi area, he is still unaware. However, he is scheduled to arrive in Tangshan within a few days, and they will meet each other. He must have confirmation that Su has resigned as the Public Security Bureau Chief of Shanhaiguan before he can appoint someone. After assuming office, he will return to Beiping and then go to Baoding, and after returning, he will inspect the administration of the various counties in his area. (3rd Day Special Dispatch)

(Tianjin) Tao Shangming finished handing over the post of Administrative Commissioner of the Ao-Yu area and went to Beiping on the evening of the 3rd. Yin Rugeng summoned the magistrates of Luan, Chang, Lu, Le, Qian, and Zun counties to Tangshan to begin discussing joint bandit suppression and defense on the 4th. (3rd Day Special Dispatch)

Commander Umezu Visits Cheng Ke Yesterday to Say Farewell 15

(Tianjin) Umezu visited Cheng Ke on the 3rd to say farewell, and is scheduled to go to Beiping within a few days to bid farewell to Wang Kemin, Bao Wen-yue, etc. (3rd Day Special Dispatch)

Takahashi Goes to Jin to Meet Yan 16

(Tianjin) According to a telegram from Baoding, Takahashi, the military attaché of the Japanese embassy in Beiping, arrived in Baoding on the 2nd and immediately visited Shang Zhen. A banquet was held for lunch, and the various departments and commissions entertained him in the evening. Early in the morning on the 3rd, Takahashi transferred to Shijiazhuang and went to Jin to meet with Yan. Takahashi claimed that this trip was for travel and there was no special mission. (3rd Day Special Dispatch)

(Beiping) Takahashi flew to Baoding on the morning of the 2nd to meet with Shang Zhen. Shang held a banquet for Takahashi in the evening. It was decided that he would go to Shijiazhuang in the afternoon of the 3rd and then to Taiyuan to meet with Yan. It is said that relations between China and Japan have become increasingly friendly, so this trip has no mission and is a private visit. (2nd Day Special Dispatch)

(Beiping) Zhu Shiqin went to Tianjin yesterday to meet with Sakai to discuss something. He returned to Beiping this afternoon after finishing the matter. (3rd Day Special Dispatch)

Numerous Foreign Warships Anchored Off the Coast of Qinhuangdao 17

(Tianjin) One British warship arrived off the coast of Qinhuangdao on the 2nd. At the same time, three destroyers of the Japanese 15th Destroyer Division arrived. Together with the French and Italian warships that arrived a few days ago, more than ten warships are now anchored in the sea. (3rd Day Special Dispatch)

Kailuan Mining Bureau Implements One Day Off Per Week 18

(Tianjin) The Kailuan Mining Bureau implemented a one-day-off-per-week system for the first time on the 2nd. Special security was enforced in all five mines to prevent worker opposition. Zhao Gezhuang was scheduled to take a day off that day, and the miners had no objection and the day passed peacefully. Wei Zichun, the manager of the mining bureau, went to Qinhuangdao on the evening of the 2nd to inspect the coal reserves and planned to find ways to promote sales. (3rd Day Special Dispatch)

Lin Shiqing and Others Arrive in Guangdong to Report on Their Trip to Europe 19

(Hong Kong) Lin Shiqing, Huang Zhiwen, Zhang Meixin, and others arrived in the province from Hong Kong on the morning of the 3rd to report to Chen Jitang on their trip to Europe. (3rd Day Special Dispatch)

Test Flight of Shaanxi-Chengdu Line Encounters Wind and Lands in Wuhan 20

(Hankou) The test flight of the Eurasia Aviation Shaanxi-Chengdu line was carried out on the 3rd, flying from Xi'an via Hanzhong to Chengdu. When passing Hanzhong at noon, it was obstructed by the wind and could not fly south, so it turned to land in Wuhan. The official opening is scheduled for the 10th. (3rd Day Special Dispatch)

Page 4

Key to British Far East Policy: The Hong Kong Governorship Issue; Criticism from Hong Kong Newspapers 21

(Hong Kong) The Shanghai *North China Daily News* recently suggested that the position of Governor of Hong Kong should be filled by a highly qualified politician who, without reducing the powers of the British ambassadors to China and Japan, would also be responsible for reporting on Pacific affairs to the British government, so that Britain would have a clear course of action. The *South China Morning Post* and *Hong Kong Telegraph* both published articles criticizing this today. The *South China Morning Post* stated that the suggestion that the Governor of Hong Kong should be a highly qualified politician, not only an administrator but also a diplomat, is extremely stimulating. This suggestion is in direct contradiction with reality. The *North China Daily News* seems to blame the people of Hong Kong for not fulfilling their responsibility in promoting Sino-British friendship. While we admit that Hong Kong has continued to offend the Chinese in certain social events, this is more the fault of the British in Hong Kong than the fault of the Colonial Office. However, these events are limited to the spiritual aspect. As for material cooperation, Hong Kong has repeatedly expressed its wishes in recent years, but China has not responded. This is also something that Shanghai should know. Hong Kong's encouragement is neither short-sighted nor factual. Hong Kong is British territory and is governed by British law. British law conflicts with Chinese law in many ways. This situation has not been fully understood by Shanghai. Moreover, Hong Kong is a naval station and an army garrison. The psychology of both Hong Kong and China is often dominated by this. This fact forces Hong Kong to remain in a transcendent and independent position. If one wants to break this, one can only change the color of the place. The psychology of the *North China Daily News* seems to be that the British government uses Hong Kong as a base to try to preserve British influence in China in order to prevent its complete extinction. If this is the case, Hong Kong's responsibility is even greater, and the position of Governor seems to be beyond the capabilities of someone who can only adapt to circumstances. The person must have sufficient talent to manage state affairs in addition to handling municipal problems, which is not easy to find. Furthermore, it is impossible for the Governor to hold the positions of diplomat and government reporter without reducing the powers of the ambassadors to Nanjing and Tokyo. Therefore, even if Hong Kong values the suggestion of the *North China Daily News* and considers it to have value, it will be regarded as an impractical plan. Ten years ago, Hong Kong had a governor who was fond of politics, resulting in mere conflicts. If Hong Kong were to implement the plan of the *North China Daily News*, it would seem better to reduce the positions of the ambassadors in Nanjing and Tokyo to consul generals rather than making the Governor of Hong Kong a super ambassador. The editorial in the *Hong Kong Telegraph* stated that the *North China Daily News*'s advocacy of a highly qualified politician to serve as Governor of Hong Kong is like whipping a dead horse. This kind of advocacy is not new, but it does not take into account reality. The suggestion that the Governor should also hold diplomatic positions in China and Japan forgets that Hong Kong is only a port for navigation and a clearinghouse for the South China market. Hong Kong's contact with China is mostly in Guangzhou. Currently, the relationship between Hong Kong and Guangzhou is better than before. The *North China Daily News* accuses Hong Kong of short-sighted isolation, but this isolation is not accurate and is far less influential than the psychology of Shanghai. Shanghai's psychology often fails to be the isolation of neutral and good relations. Under general issues, Hong Kong does not need to separate from the management of the Colonial Office, nor is there a reason to think that this kind of change is feasible. The Colonial Office has already decided on the Governor's figure. If special circumstances require the connection of the Hong Kong government with diplomatic duties, the plan for the exchange of opinions that is required already exists. (3rd Day Reuters Dispatch)

Chahar Provincial Government Sends Additional Personnel to Rescue Jones; Qin Dechun Cables Instructions to Ensure a Swift Rescue 22

(Beiping) This afternoon, a telephone call was received in Beiping from Zhangjiakou, stating that at 5:00 AM this morning, the Chahar Provincial Government sent two more important officials from Zhangjiakou by car to Baochang, along with Platoon Leader Zhang of the Baochang Security Team, who had previously accompanied the German reporter Miller to escape. They will all go to the bandit den to rescue the British reporter Jones. Due to heavy rain in the Zhangbei area, the car is moving very slowly. The officials are expected to reach their destination tonight or tomorrow morning to discuss everything with the bandits. There should be concrete results tomorrow. The rumor that Jones has been freed and has returned to Beiping via Toronto is incorrect. The German reporter Miller had agreed with Jones and the bandit leader when leaving the bandit den that he would be responsible for negotiating with our country's officials to redeem Jones. Therefore, Miller left Beiping again for Zhangjiakou last night, arriving at 2:00 AM this morning. He consulted with the Chahar authorities and the British military officer Moore, who is now in Zhangjiakou, and it was decided that this afternoon he would go from Zhangjiakou to Baochang and then to the bandit den, accompanied by the personnel sent by the Provincial Government and Platoon Leader Zhang, to contact the bandits. Wang Kemin sent a long letter to Qin Dechun this morning, stating in the original letter that British reporter Jones is a [associate] of David Lloyd George and has a high position, so please try your best to find a way to get him out of danger as soon as possible. After receiving the letter, Qin immediately informed Yang Nan, the secretary-general of the Chahar Provincial Government, by long-distance telephone, instructing him to rescue Jones, and the bandits' demands could be considered and handled as appropriate within the possible scope. According to reports from foreigners, the bandits have now moved Jones to a mountain more than ten miles from the original den to hide him, in order to avoid official attention. (3rd Day Special Dispatch)

(Beiping) Miller telegraphed to Beiping that the bandits seemed to have moved Jones to a certain place near the Rehe border, but the negotiation location for the representatives sent by the Chinese authorities to negotiate with the bandits is still near Baochang. (2nd Day Special Dispatch)

(Beiping) According to news from Zhangjiakou this morning, Jones' ransom has been sent from Zhangjiakou to Baochang. The amount is unknown. It is now hoped that Jones can get out of danger tomorrow or on Sunday. It is heard that the kidnappers have moved Jones to a certain location fifty miles east of Baochang, near the Rehe border. The people sent by the Chahar Provincial Government to contact the bandits have met with the bandits a few miles east of Guyuan. According to the latest news, the bandits have reduced the amount of the ransom to 10,000 yuan, which proves that the bandits now feel that the hostage is a burden. However, the troops have not coerced them to move Jones far away, which is puzzling. (3rd Day Reuters Telegram)

Hammond Arrives in Nanjing to Report on Railway Inspection 23

(Nanjing) Hammond visited Zeng Zhongming, Lu Xinchou, and others at the Ministry of Railways in the afternoon to report on the railway inspection. Hai's term of office in China is set for three months and will expire at the end of this month. After the report and general recommendations are completed, he will return to England next month. (3rd Day Special Dispatch)

(Nanjing) British railway expert General Hammond, accompanied by Zheng Baozhao, deputy director of the Beining Railway, arrived in Nanjing by China Aviation Corporation airplane at noon on the 3rd. We attacked several times, but the bandits resisted stubbornly. After nightfall, we divided our troops and used local guides to attack their rear, cutting off the bandits' retreat. The bandits increased their troops and charged with all their might, but our officers and soldiers remained calm and executed a fierce frontal attack. The bandits were unable to hold out and retreated toward Xiaoba. They are currently under pursuit. Beichuan City has now been officially recaptured. Among them, five are large money shops and four are small and medium-sized money shops. It is estimated that more than twenty money shops in Ningbo have closed, and only about ten are still operating normally. Current Affairs Commentary

Two Principles Regarding the Upbringing of Children 40

— Du

The nationally designated Year of the Child began on August 1st. The entire nation has united to enthusiastically promote it. Its grand scale is universally admired. Truly, children are the future masters of the nation, the linchpin of the nation's rise and fall. If we wish to secure the foundation of the nation, we must prioritize laying a solid foundation. Now, with the advocacy of the party and government authorities above and the implementation by local agencies below, and with the establishment of implementation committees everywhere to jointly plan for the well-being of children, and with the talent and effort of the entire nation over the years, we will surely be able to formulate practical steps to serve as a general standard for progress. How fortunate are these young scholars to encounter this favorable time, to sharpen their minds and take advantage of the momentum to rise up. The brilliance of their future will be limitless.

Regarding plans for children's education, the discussions of prominent figures and the designs of experts should not lack grand strategies and sound advice that can be followed. Here, I offer my humble opinion on the principles of implementation.

First, with regard to the aspect of cultivation, we should establish appropriate norms. Children are innocent and unblemished, with unrestrained emotions. They become red or black depending entirely on their surroundings. A careless beginning makes a successful ending difficult to achieve. Therefore, under the supervision of teachers, guardians, fathers, and elder brothers, we should strive to avoid negative impressions. Just as pure buds should be carefully protected in every way, we must not allow them to be stained by muddy soil. The distinction between good and evil, and the evaluation of superior and inferior, can be repeatedly presented and subtly explained by adults at any time. What is fairness? What is baseness? What is integrity? What is treachery? This will allow children to develop a sound concept of personality and prevent them from easily wavering in their principles in the future. Teachers should take this as the goal of moral education, and fathers and elder brothers should especially serve as role models for the young. However, if we adults reflect on the past, we will truly feel ashamed when facing the children. We ask ourselves honestly, even if we have not actively committed evil deeds, we have inevitably neglected to prevent evil from occurring. The people are the masters of the country. Have we truly fulfilled our responsibilities as masters, even in a small way? Leaving other things aside, the existence of a cowardly mentality is already an indelible testament to our guilt. And yet we dare to speak of being role models? Do we not feel ashamed? To make amends for the past, we can only resolutely confess our faults and point out the gains and losses, so that the future masters of the nation will clearly understand the duties of a citizen, and so that they will not repeat the mistakes of fear and hesitation. If we can learn from our mistakes, there is still hope for redemption. It is not too late to make amends.

Second, with regard to the aspect of enlightenment, we should be based entirely on science. The need for children's education to be based on science is not only for the sake of their academic future, but also essential for their general reasoning ability. In the past, there was no lack of intelligent and eloquent youth, but when it came to distinguishing between emotions and reason, it was always difficult to expect accurate understanding. Numerical statistics were carelessly approximate, and the distinction between right and wrong often involved ambiguity. All these errors in judgment are due to the lack of scientific concepts. Children generally inherit these qualities, and it is difficult to eliminate them because they are deeply ingrained. If their education from the beginning is based on science, then as a result of gradual and reasoned explanations, it will not be difficult for them to gradually develop clear minds. The benefits to their future understanding will be more than just a small improvement. Furthermore, books that contradict scientific principles and could hinder the development of children's thinking should be strictly prohibited and absolutely not allowed to be read. This will reduce the unexpected harm and promote overall progress.

The above two points require the joint efforts of fathers, elder brothers, and teachers, and should consider both moral cultivation and academic knowledge to create a majority of good young people. On the one hand, this will cultivate the future pillars of the country, and on the other hand, it will wash away our past sins. At the beginning of the Year of the Child, I dare to express this idea, which those with a sense of responsibility should not ignore.

Japanese Government Issues Statement Clarifying National Polity, Forcefully Rejects the Theory of the Emperor as an Organ of State, Army Authorities Express Satisfaction 43

Okada Discusses the Advancement or Retreat of the Privy Council President and Director-General of the Legislation Bureau

(Tokyo) The government issued a statement clarifying the national polity at 1:00 PM on the afternoon of the 3rd. The full text is as follows: The national polity of Japan was manifested in the divine decree issued when the Heavenly Grandson descended upon this country, that is, that the Emperor of an unbroken line reigns over the country, and the prosperity of the imperial lineage is as limitless as heaven and earth. At the time of the promulgation of the Constitution, Emperor Meiji issued an edict stating, "The great authority to govern the country, I inherit from my ancestors, and transmit to my descendants." Furthermore, Article 1 of the Constitution stipulates, "The Emperor of Japan reigns over and governs the Empire of Japan in an unbroken line." That the great authority to govern Japan clearly resides in the Emperor is quite evident. However, to assume that the authority to govern does not reside in the Emperor, but that the Emperor is merely an organ for exercising the authority to govern, is contrary to the unique essence of the Japanese national polity. Recently, there have been various discussions on constitutional theory regarding the essence of the national polity, which is deeply regrettable. The government hereby dedicates itself to clarifying the national polity, in order to reveal its essence. It earnestly hopes that all parties will cooperate to this end. This is hereby declared. (3rd day Domei dispatch)

(Tokyo) Prime Minister Okada issued a statement saying that the government has already clarified the national polity. It is said that the President of the Privy Council, Ikkii Kitokuro, is a proponent of the organ theory. However, Mr. Ikkii studied national law 34 years ago and spoke of the position of the Japanese Emperor. Since entering the Imperial Court, he has detached himself from the position and learning of a scholar and has reached this point today. Therefore, there is no possibility of the issue of Mr. Ikkii's advancement or retreat arising. It has also been rumored that the Director-General of the Legislation Bureau, Mr. Kanemori, will resign. However, I am confident that Mr. Kanemori is by no means a proponent of the organ theory, so there is no possibility of his resignation. As for the disposition of other scholars who advocate the organ theory and their writings, the authorities of the Ministry of Home Affairs will resolve it in accordance with the policy decided by the Cabinet. (3rd day United Press dispatch)

(Tokyo) The army authorities expressed satisfaction with the government's issuance of the statement. The text advocating the rejection of the organ theory, etc., as advocated by the army and navy, has been adopted in the statement, and the attitude has been clarified. It can be seen that the government is truly sincere on this issue. However, the issuance of the statement is only one means of rejecting the organ theory and clarifying the national polity. There will be opportunities in the future to thoroughly resolve this issue in order to clarify the national polity. (3rd day Domei dispatch)

(Tokyo) The government firmly believes that the issuance of the statement clarifying the national polity will resolve the theory of the Emperor as an organ of state, which has been a problem in political circles for the past half year. When the initial movement to reject the organ theory was at its height, the government recognized that there were unsavory elements with the aim of overthrowing the cabinet, and therefore maintained a cautious attitude toward all matters. Recently, the army and navy have actively demanded that this issue be resolved, and because the future appears promising, it has decided to issue the statement. Now that the hopes of the military have been realized, it is expected that there is no possibility of this issue developing further. (3rd day Domei dispatch)

Army Minister to Meet Matsuoka, Instruct on Manchurian Policy, Tada Scheduled to Go to Tianjin 44

(Tokyo) Army Minister Hayashi will go to Hokkaido around the 12th for inspection. Before his departure, he plans to meet with Matsuoka, President of the South Manchuria Railway, in his capacity as the Director-General of the Manchurian Affairs Bureau, to instruct him on the policies to be implemented toward Manchuria. The main points are roughly as follows:

(1) Since the reform of the Manchurian institutions, the political structure of Japan in Manchuria has been controlled by the Commander of the Kwantung Army and the Ambassador Extraordinary and Plenipotentiary, and it is now entering a period of activity in economic, industrial, and construction projects.

(2) The South Manchuria Railway has a major mission for economic, industrial, and construction projects in Manchuria. The president and leading personnel should be aware of the importance of their mission, stand from the perspective of the nation, and implement management affairs.

(3) In implementing industrial construction projects in Manchuria, it is first necessary to reorganize the South Manchuria Railway to adapt to the new situation after the Manchurian Incident. The new president must study this point and communicate with various local agencies in order to implement the fundamental national policy. (3rd day Domei dispatch)

(Tokyo) The new Commander of the Japanese Army in China, Major General Tada, is scheduled to leave Tokyo for his post on the 9th and arrive in Tianjin on the 16th. Umezu will succeed him in office. Umezu is scheduled to return to Japan on the 21st. (3rd day Domei dispatch)

Russian Aviator Takes Off in the Rain, Moscow to San Francisco, Non-Stop Route over the Arctic, Paving a New Path for American-Russian Friendship 50

(Moscow) The famous Soviet aviator Levanevsky, along with two companions, took off from Moscow at 6:00 this morning aboard a single-engine aircraft, heading directly to San Francisco via the Arctic, with no stops along the way. The American ambassador to Russia, Bullitt, and senior Soviet officials were at the airfield to see them off. Levanevsky's plane carried a stove for use in case of a forced landing over the Arctic Ocean. In addition, 40 meteorological stations have been specially set up in the Arctic region to provide Levanevsky with real-time reference information. As Levanevsky took off, it was pouring rain. However, when the plane was 150 kilometers away, it radioed back that the weather was very clear. If there are no obstacles, it should be able to fly to San Francisco within 70 hours. (3rd day Kuomintang Central News Agency dispatch)

(Moscow) Soviet aviator Levanevsky has now flown out of Russia and plans to reach San Francisco via the Arctic. The Soviet authorities hope to establish a regular air route between Russia and the United States via the Arctic in the future. It is reported that Levanevsky is carrying sufficient equipment and food. If he is unfortunately forced to land in the Arctic, he can at least sustain his life for three months. A team of icebreakers and several aircraft are concentrated in the Arctic Ocean, ready to go to his aid as soon as a distress call is received.

(Continuation) Levanevsky flew to the Barents Sea, the southeastern corner of the Arctic Ocean, at 12:25. (3rd day Reuters dispatch)

(Moscow) The aircraft flying directly from Moscow to San Francisco has only one engine, with 950 horsepower. There are three crew members in total. The plane weighs 11 tons, including gasoline. The range of the plane is 8,100 kilometers, while the distance from Moscow to San Francisco is only 6,250 kilometers. (3rd day Kuomintang Central News Agency dispatch)

(Seattle) According to a report from the Meteorological Observatory today, the Soviet aviator crossing the Arctic will probably encounter haze when flying over American territory. A telegram from Alaska also stated that the area is currently covered in dense clouds. It is generally expected that the Soviet aviator may take an inland route directly to San Francisco. (2nd day Kuomintang Central News Agency dispatch)

(Moscow) As Soviet aviator Levanevsky is about to undertake a flight from Moscow to San Francisco via the Arctic, American Ambassador to the Soviet Union Bullitt declared that he hopes Levanevsky's heroic flight can pave a new path for friendship between the American and Soviet people. (3rd day TASS dispatch)

Details of Russian Plane's Departure: Extremely Tight Security at the Airfield 51

(Moscow) The famous Soviet aviator Captain Levanevsky plans to fly an airplane through the Arctic directly to the United States to open up a regular air and mail route between Russia and the United States via the Arctic. Preparations have been underway for some time, and he departed at 6:00 this morning, accompanied by Bedugov and Lekinko, from the Churchikov airfield, 40 kilometers from here, heading to San Francisco. Only a very small number of people were granted permission to enter the airfield at that time. Journalists were invited to come at 1:00 PM. By 3:00 AM, military police had driven around the airfield three times for security, and the entire airfield was still shrouded in darkness. By 4:00 AM, the east gradually began to brighten, and then two aircraft were seen rising into the air. They were test flights. At that time, within 150 kilometers of Moscow, there was heavy rain. Levanevsky's plane was carrying 7,200 liters of gasoline and 500 kilograms of engine oil. The weight was considerable, and flying in the rain was dangerous. Therefore, people at the airfield were anxious, fearing that Levanevsky's heroic feat would be hampered by the rain and unable to be completed. Just as they were hesitating, news came that Levanevsky had decided to take off. The whole airfield cheered. At that time, People's Commissar for Defense Voroshilov, People's Commissar for Internal Affairs Yezhov, and the American Ambassador to Russia Bullitt and his wife were talking with the three aviators to be sent off next to the plane. At 5:45 AM, the engine of the plane started to turn. At 6:00, a signal to leave the airfield was given. At 6:05, the plane started to move. Twenty minutes later, looking at the plane from afar, it was in good condition, soaring straight into the clouds. This flight will cover 3,000 kilometers over land and several thousand kilometers over the sea. At the beginning of the flight, the speed will not exceed 150 kilometers per hour. But along the way, as the gasoline is gradually consumed, the weight of the plane will decrease, and the speed will also increase accordingly. The plane is a monoplane with extremely long wings, reaching 40 meters. The plane body is painted red, and the cockpit is extremely small, hidden in the huge fuselage, making it almost impossible to distinguish from a distance. (3rd day Havas dispatch)

Outer Mongolia Refuses to Exchange Diplomatic Representatives with the Puppet Organization 52

(Changchun) The government of Outer Mongolia officially replied to the "Manchukuo" government on the 29th, refusing to exchange diplomatic representatives. (3rd day Domei dispatch)

Abyssinia Also Expresses Acceptance of the British-French Draft, Representatives of League of Nations Countries are Preparing Speeches 53

(Addis Ababa) The Ethiopian King told a Reuters reporter this afternoon that he had instructed his representative in Geneva, Haile Hawariat, to sign the resolution drafted by Eden and Laval so that the Italo-Ethiopian dispute could be resolved peacefully. (3rd day Reuters dispatch)

(Geneva) Attention in Geneva is now focused on the Ethiopian representative, Haile Hawariat. Many people gathered in front of his hotel today, hoping to catch a glimpse of this short, dark-skinned, mustachioed gentleman leaving the hotel. A team of film cameramen was also on standby, hoping to capture his image. Haile Hawariat is currently in close consultation with his legal counsel, Dr. Juraj Ghyczy. Multiple coded telegrams are on his desk. They are awaiting instructions from Addis Ababa. Even if a telegram arrives approving the resolution, the heart of the problem still needs to be dealt with by the British, French, and Italian representatives in France. The current procedures only move the situation slightly forward. The Council of the League of Nations is expected to meet at 5:00 PM this afternoon, but the time may have to be changed. Most representatives are now preparing their speeches, and Eden's speech is particularly important. The Ethiopian representative's speech is also of great interest. Litvinov's declaration on the negotiations between the United Kingdom, France, and Italy has not yet been finalized, as the Ethiopian representative may make a statement, so it may have to be delayed slightly. (3rd day Reuters dispatch)

(Geneva) The public meeting of the Council of the League of Nations, which was originally scheduled to convene at 10:00 AM today, has been postponed to the afternoon because the Ethiopian representative needs to request instructions from Addis Ababa regarding the newly established mediation method, and because the British representative requested that the British government be given the opportunity to carefully consider several key points. (3rd day Kuomintang Central News Agency dispatch)

(Geneva) A complete compromise was reached last night on the resolution concerning the Italo-Ethiopian dispute that will be submitted to the Council of the League of Nations. The resolution will be submitted to the Council meeting this afternoon after receiving the Ethiopian government's reply. It stipulates (1) the resumption of mediation on the case of the Walwal clashes; (2) the appointment of a fifth arbitrator; (3) the Council will reconvene on September 4 to discuss the entire issue. The second section of the resolution refers to the Council's resolution of May 25 regarding the resolution of the dispute being implemented in accordance with Article 5 of the 1928 treaty (this is to implicitly include the declaration not to resort to force). Council Chairman Litvinov will read a declaration today concerning the fact that the three countries, namely the United Kingdom, France, and Italy, are willing to negotiate in accordance with the 1906 treaty. One of the biggest difficulties now is that the United Kingdom insists that the League of Nations should negotiate with Italy in accordance with the 1906 treaty. Yesterday afternoon, responsible parties stated that the differences between the three major countries, the United Kingdom, France, and Italy, have been reconciled to the point where complete harmony can be expected within 12 hours, so all parties are optimistic that a compromise can be achieved. The Council was originally scheduled to meet last night, but was temporarily canceled. After negotiations, the differences between the United Kingdom and Italy remain only a minor matter regarding the reference clause, which should not be difficult to resolve. Italian Prime Minister Mussolini indicated in a telegram that Italy is willing to abide by the resolution. (3rd day Reuters dispatch)

(London) According to a report from the Times correspondent in Addis Ababa, the people of Addis Ababa felt disappointed and heartbroken after receiving news from Geneva. Some even thought that Ethiopia had been fooled and had lost its original position in the League of Nations. This is because Ethiopia's appeal to the League of Nations was based on the provisions of the Covenant, but now it is advocating negotiations based on the 1906 treaty between the United Kingdom, France, and Italy regarding Ethiopia, which has disappointed the expectations of Ethiopia. The correspondent also said that the Ethiopian Emperor may issue a new declaration and issue new instructions to the representatives attending the Council meeting. (3rd day Havas dispatch)

Mussolini Continues to Move Troops to East Africa; Three Thousand Sick Soldiers Carried Back at Night 54

(Rome) On July 6th, Italian Prime Minister Mussolini delivered a warning-filled speech to the Blackshirts, in which he said, "You are invincible; you will soon see the five continents bend and tremble before the power of Fascism." The full text of his speech has just been released to newspapers, but the newspapers only carried the main points. Mussolini also said, "You are about to go to Abyssinia, and the entire territory of Abyssinia will belong to you. If the Abyssinians resist our terrible power, we will subject them to burning and plunder. We will slap the cheeks of the white protectors among the blacks and retaliate." (Reuters, 3rd)

(Rome) Italians believe that Abyssinia is Mussolini's trump card. He is determined to stake everything on it. If he wins in one fell swoop, he will be remembered in history, and future generations will view his martial prowess as surpassing Caesar. If he fails, Italian politics will undergo a complete new orientation. The outcome is of great importance, and the entire psychology of the Fascist Party is now focused on this. Therefore, the strategies employed by the League of Nations and Britain and France through the 1906 treaty cannot prevent Italy from gambling on this victory or defeat. The Italian attitude towards Abyssinia can be seen from this. (Reuters, 3rd)

(Paris) According to a dispatch from Naples today, two Italian ships arrived at night, carrying back three thousand sick soldiers from African colonies. They were then quietly distributed to various hospitals in Italy. At the same time, a laborer who had just returned to Italy from Africa reported that Commander-in-Chief Graziani severely threatened those who complained. It was also said that for those who were sick, their daily pay was reduced by two lire. The discipline in the colonies is even stricter than in the early days of the Fascist civilian army. The return of the sick soldiers has slightly dampened the courage of the citizens who are scheduled to depart. (Reuters, 3rd)

(Rome) The Italian government may mobilize all fourth-class soldiers at any moment, totaling approximately 800,000 men. Two army divisions, totaling 30,000 men, and the remaining soldiers from the 1912 class, totaling 150,000 men, will be officially announced today. Three ships transporting soldiers and war materials to East Africa departed from Naples today. There are also twelve ships currently busy loading troops. In addition, one or more divisions of Blackshirts will be called up before the end of this session of the League of Nations Council. This action demonstrates that Italy, regardless of the interference of the League of Nations or other parties, is vigorously pursuing its planned plan. At the same time, Italian writer Gaeda published an article in a newspaper commenting on British Foreign Secretary Hoare's speech in the House of Commons on Thursday, expressing that Italy may be forced to withdraw from the League of Nations, calling Hoare's words cowardly, and questioning whether Hoare's final section mentioning British military strength was intended to intimidate Italy. (Reuters, 2nd)

(Rome) The semi-official Italian newspaper recently published a commentary stating, "British Foreign Secretary Hoare's speech yesterday in the British House of Commons regarding the Italian-Abyssinian dispute was quite strong in tone and even carried a hint of intimidation. This speech shows that Britain's current policy toward Italy has taken an openly hostile attitude. Hoare's speech does not contribute to the peaceful resolution of the Italian-Abyssinian dispute; on the contrary, it spreads a cloud over British-Italian relations, and it will be very difficult to dispel this cloud." The newspaper then pointed out the following three points: "(1) The 1915 Secret Treaty of London between Britain, France, and Italy allowed Italy to expand its colonies, but Italy was rejected during the signing of the peace treaty after the war and could not obtain Germany's pre-war colonies. Now that Britain is unwilling to propose to the League of Nations to amend the mandate system, Italy can only seek colonies on its own. (2) Italy has not taken a stand against the League of Nations; it only opposes Britain's interpretation of the League of Nations Covenant. If Italy is forced to withdraw from the League of Nations over the Abyssinian issue, it would be a serious blow to the collective security plan. (3) We acknowledge that France has repeatedly voiced support for Italy; what we are now paying attention to is that France will surely clarify the situation." (Havas, 2nd)

Egyptian Muslims Hold Anti-Italian Demonstrations; Italians Try to Win Back Public Opinion 55

Alexandria: The local Muslim Youth Association held an anti-Italian demonstration, demanding that Eastern countries organize a support association for Abyssinia's independence struggle. The association's committee also declared to the League of Nations and various countries that Italy is now pursuing its imperialist policies. Former Minister of the Army and Egypt's most famous Muslim, Taff Ta'sani, was an important Egyptian figure who participated in this demonstration. According to those close to the Abyssinian side, the number of retired Egyptian military officers requesting to enlist in the service is increasing daily. (National Telegram, 2nd)

Alexandria: Italians here are now doing their best to win Egyptian public opinion over to Italy, hoping to dispel the various sympathies that the Egyptian people have recently expressed towards Abyssinia. The British here are greatly disturbed by an article published in a Fascist newspaper, which first described Italy's peaceful intentions towards Abyssinia, and then described Italy's long-standing friendship with Egypt, urging the Egyptian people not to deeply believe the criticisms of others, because in their eyes, pacifying Abyssinia is tantamount to losing a prize. The article's anti-British sentiment is very obvious, stating that Italy will protect Abyssinia, so that it will not be harmed by those with ambition, because these people, although they have already obtained Sudan and have ruled the Nile River basin, are still not satisfied. (National Telegram, 3rd)

Japanese Activity in Tianjin; Economic Cooperation 84

Establishment of North China Rural Relief Association and International Bank Branch

Tianjin Correspondence: It has recently been widely rumored here that Gao Lingrui, the former Minister of Internal Affairs of the Northern Government, and Wang Shuangqi and other gentlemen in Tianjin, have initiated the organization of the North China Rural Relief Committee, with the aim of developing transportation, water conservancy, minerals, and agricultural crops in Hebei and Chahar. The funds will be provided by the Japanese International Bank, and the Japanese propaganda says that this move is another way for Sino-Japanese economic cooperation. However, Gao Lingrui has recently troubled his friends to unofficially deny the rumors to the newspapers, saying that Japanese friends have indeed exchanged opinions on this in private conversations, and he has only discussed it slightly from an objective standpoint and has not immediately agreed with any party or person to determine how to cooperate. However, denials were made, but rumors continue. It is difficult to make a judgment on the truth of the event. The Japanese International Bank, whose headquarters is located in Tokyo, has now sent Director Shohtaro Yoshihara and Deputy Chief Sakamura to Tianjin to prepare for the establishment of a branch. The address has been found at 34 Fazu Street in the Meiye Building. It is scheduled to start operating unofficially in late August. Gu Yuan and Sakamura are currently engaged in activities related to Sino-Japanese economic cooperation, contacting banks, industrialists, and influential military and political figures in Tianjin and Beiping who have huge amounts of capital, hoping to cooperate with the goal of developing resources, abandoning government relations. Quite a few people believe in their saying, and they are constantly negotiating with each other. It is heard that the funds for the branch are planned to be independent, set at US$15 million. In addition to the Japanese capital invested by the headquarters, some Chinese capital will also be raised in North China as the Chinese representative capital. This plan, the Sino-Japanese economic cooperation discussed by Chinese and Japanese economic industrialists in the Jiashu Society in the British Concession of Tianjin on the 25th and 26th of last month, has the same purpose. Because although the Japanese are currently advocating Sino-Japanese economic cooperation, they require too much money, and if they want to realize their plan in one fell swoop, the facts are not possible, and their financial resources are also insufficient. Therefore, they are pulling out Chinese private capital, nominally cooperating, so as to proceed quickly. It is also the unanimous opinion of the Japanese Kwantung Army Department, the North China Garrison Department, and the South Manchuria Railway. Since the middle of last month, the South Manchuria Railway Company and the Shenyang Japanese Industry and Commerce North China Investigation Group have sent people to work in Tianjin, Beiping, Hebei, Chahar, Shandong, and Suiyuan. In addition to most of the group members investigating relevant materials and returning to Dalian and Shenyang, there are still a few group members working in Tianjin, Baoding, Shijiazhuang, and other areas, such as measuring the Hai River and investigating the import and export cargo figures and types of customs. It is heard that the Japanese intend to deepen the Hai River in the name of Sino-Japanese economic cooperation so that cargo ships of more than 2,000 tons can directly reach Tianjin. They also plan to invest in the construction of a lateral railway connecting the Jinpu and Pinghan lines, starting from Cang County on the Jinpu line and reaching Shijiazhuang on the Pinghan line. If necessary, they may extend the Cang County area and build it to Dagu and Geju under the sea, as the two major land and water transportation lines. In addition, there is a plan to connect the Pinghan and Jiaoji lines, but the starting and ending points have not yet been determined. (1st)

Bandit Troubles in Hebei Province: Plan to Divide into Three Areas for Vigorous Suppression 85

Over Forty Counties Report Bandit Troubles, Shang Zhen Plans to Advance and Suppress

Baoding Correspondence: Hebei Province Chairman Shang Zhen recently went from Baoding to Ping to meet with Wang Kemin to report on provincial administration since taking office, and made some requests. He then went to Tianjin to handle matters at the Tianjin-Gu Security Headquarters. On the 29th of last month, he returned to Baoding from Ping. He then summoned all the department heads at his residence to discuss financial and bandit suppression issues in the province. Bandit troubles have occurred frequently in the province, with over forty counties reporting bandit activity. The bandit situation in Wen'an and Ba Counties has recently become particularly rampant. He believes that unless bandit troubles are cleared up, the people cannot live in peace. Therefore, he plans to divide the province into three areas: north, south, and central. He will also transfer strong troops to organize three bandit suppression detachments to carry out vigorous suppression, with the aim of clearing them out as soon as possible. As for the bandits in the reed marshes of Wen'an and Ba Counties, Song Kentang's troops are currently handling the suppression. The reed marshes in that area are deep and extensive, and the air inside is foul. Many soldiers become dizzy after entering. The method of attack has now been changed, and then a general offensive will be ordered. It is expected that they can be completely eliminated soon. In addition, the province's financial deficit is huge. Transportation between Ping, Baoding, and Tianjin is being actively reorganized. All telephone lines and highways will be repaired soon, and so on. After Shang's remarks, he went to the provincial government. That evening, he summoned Finance Director Li Jingrong at his private residence to discuss how to reorganize the province's finances until late at night.

Inspection Report on Flood Disaster Along Rivers 86

— (Special Correspondent Ya of This Newspaper)

Tracing Up the Xiang River

This Yangtze River flood has been most devastating to Hubei Province. Among the counties in Hubei Province, those in the Xiang River basin have suffered the most severely. The Xiang River originates from the Panlong Mountain in Shaanxi and passes through Hanzhong (Nanzheng), so it is also known as the Han River. It flows eastward in a winding course, and all the waters of northern Sichuan and southern Shaanxi flow into it. Upon entering Hubei, it also receives the Du River, Dan River, Nan River, and San River. When it flows to Xiangyang and Fancheng, the large Bai River also joins it. It meanders southeastward and flows into the Yangtze River, a distance of over three thousand li. From Xiangfan downstream, the counties it passes through, such as Yicheng, Zhongxiang, Qianjiang, Jingshan, Mianyang, Tianmen, Hanchuan, and Hanyang, are only fifty meters above sea level. The land is flat and unobstructed, with interconnected lakes and streams. When one river swells and one dike breaks, nearby areas are invariably affected. Shaanxi has always been known as a drought-prone province, but this summer there has been continuous heavy rain. The Xiang River, which collects all the waters south of the Qinling Mountains, surges and rushes downstream to Chu. Initially, it overflowed in Yunxi, Gucheng, and Xiangfan, and the damage was limited to the areas along the banks. Subsequently, the Shuanghe Dike (belonging to Tianmen County) and the Shizi Estuary (belonging to Zhongxiang County, located between Maliang and Jiukou, also known as San Si Gong and Longwang Temple, upstream of Shuanghe Estuary, which breached one day after Shuanghe Dike) successively collapsed. Interconnecting and crisscrossing, the water rose more than ten feet above the ground, completely submerging the entire territory of Tianmen, Hanchuan, and Hanyang, as well as large parts of Jingshan, Yingcheng, Xiaogan, Huangpi, Qianjiang, and Mianyang, in a vast expanse of floodwaters. At that time, how the flood torrents came like shaking mountains and moving peaks, how the villages collapsed and drifted away, how the disaster-stricken people cried to heaven without response and appealed to earth without recourse, not knowing how to struggle painfully, and finally drowned and died. We all belong to the same species, the same nation with shared joys and sorrows. Try to close your eyes and imagine this tragedy that exhausts human misery. Shouldn't we be able to move with compassion, each with a heart to treat others' misfortune as our own, and do our best to seek good follow-up measures?

Having decided to go to the aforementioned Xiang River region to investigate, the reporter boarded a steamer from Hankou on the 27th and traced up the Xiang River. Where the river enters the Yangtze, the current is unusually rapid, with a lot of sediment mixed in. The difference in the quality and color of the water from the Yangtze is almost like the Jing and Wei Rivers. Cotton mills, flour mills, and other factories line both banks, numbering no less than thirty or forty. However, less than one-tenth of them are emitting black smoke, presumably due to economic panic or the suspension of work due to the flood. Hanyang is located at the confluence of the Yangtze and Xiang Rivers, with low-lying terrain. The rising waters of both rivers have caused disasters, and nineteen out of ten of the urban and rural areas have been flooded. More than 470,000 people have been affected, scattered and displaced, in a very miserable state. Fortunately, news of the disaster upstream was received early, and fewer people have died. However, the disaster victims have no food, and it is difficult to provide sufficient relief. In more remote villages, there have been incidents of looting for food. Like sparks starting a prairie fire, we cannot but pay close attention to this. Boats and ships ply the river like shuttles. Those going upstream mostly carry wood, bamboo from Hunan, and food. Those going downstream mostly carry furniture such as trunks, cabinets, pots, and jars, as disaster victims try to escape. Occasionally, there are boats carrying "Shigao" (a specialty of Yingcheng) and "Maling melon," all covered in yellow mud. The Xiang River basin was originally a rich agricultural area in central Hubei. In previous years, the Xiang River was a thousand miles long, transporting food and cotton to Wuhan for concentration. But now, seeing this abnormal scene, one cannot help but feel desolate. Looking to the right at the Luojia Store area where the river flows into Moon Lake, many houses have been washed away, and few people live there. Outside the dike, the water is still connected to the sky, with no end in sight. Looking to the left, the hills rise and fall, resembling islands in a deep pool. Disaster victims have built sheds and huts, stretching endlessly. The willows and distant trees on both sides of the dike, with fallen leaves, seem to be in autumn, and the fields and ridges are nowhere to be seen.

Caidian is a town in the second district of Hanyang, 60 li from Hankou. It has a large population and relatively prosperous commerce. When the floodwaters rose sharply, because the town was lower than the water level, the residents all fled to Xijia Ridge. However, those who were working in the nearby fields or were struggling to protect miscellaneous items drowned more than 200 people. The total population of the district is 130,000. Because the fields have been submerged and no harvest has been reaped, everyone is trapped in a water prison and starving village. According to the old farmers, if the water recedes quickly within half a month, it is still possible to replant mung beans and millet. If it is delayed until the end of August, it will be too late. Moreover, after the disaster this autumn, they will not be able to plant wheat, and a spring famine next year will be inevitable. Fortunately, the emergency work-relief program prepared by the Provincial Disaster Relief Association is being implemented step by step to alleviate the immediate emergency and eliminate future hidden worries.

The Huangjiadu River bends and meanders for more than twenty li. Sailboats have a shallow draft and can pass directly through the gaps between the willows on the embankment. Therefore, those far behind the steamer all rushed straight ahead. From Xuyou Caidian to Hanchuan, the water route is 120 li, but the land route is only 50 li. Also, from Hanchuan to Fanmakou, the water route is 30 li, but the land route is only 7 li. There are probably countless such bends upstream. In the future, if the river channel is dredged, bends straightened, and straightened, the benefits of eliminating harm and promoting benefits cannot be overstated. From Caidian to Huangjiadu to Xingu, the water route is 60 li. In the middle, there are two or three breaches on the left embankment, which have been flooded by lake water. The clear blue waves are distinctly different from the river water. River fish compete to welcome the lake water, making fishing very easy. The disaster victims living on the embankment, whether because they were envious of the fish in the deep water or driven by hunger, even used their clothes and pants as nets. This is also an original sight on this trip. In addition, disaster victims who are exposed to the elements often worship the clay and wooden idols they have rescued as usual, with red flags and green covers, which is quite eye-catching.

Xingu is also a town along the river in Hanyang. At this point, the waterway splits into two: one goes north to Yingcheng and Tianmen, which is the Yun River, a tributary of the Xiang River; the other goes west to Hanchuan and Mianyang, which is the main stream of the Xiang River. The steamer the reporter boarded was going to Hanchuan. There are about 2,000 residents in Xingu, about 300 households. There is a red-tiled tea house that is two or three stories taller than other houses and can be seen from dozens of miles away. It is said to have been built more than ten years ago. Now, the local economy is exhausted and there is no ability to rebuild such buildings. The Xiang River rose sharply on July 11, reaching the eaves of houses. After the 14th, it gradually receded. Although the water has now receded from the banks, many of the foundations of the houses along the river have been washed away by the flood, and the houses are suspended in the air, which is not safe to live in for a day. However, most of the house owners are disaster victims who are struggling to survive and have no way to seek other help. The streets are full of mud and sewage, and the stench is overwhelming. The scattered food sold is especially the place where flies and mosquitoes gather. After a major disaster, it is easy to suffer from the epidemic. If it is not treated early, I am afraid that the disaster victims will eventually form an inextricable relationship with death. Alas! (Xingu, July 27)

Wuhu Industry Depressed, Yuzhong Cotton Mill Suspends Operations, Declares Liquidation with 3 Million Yuan Debt, Causing Panic for Thousands of Livelihoods 87

Wuhu Correspondence: Wuhu Yuzhong Cotton Mill was founded by Li Bohang and others, and has been in operation for more than ten years. The capital reached a huge amount of one million yuan. The size of the machinery factory is the only industrial construction in Anhui Province. At the time of commencement, there were a total of one thousand four or five hundred employees and workers. Before 1929, the conditions in terms of products and sales were excellent, and there were often surpluses. Unexpectedly, since 1929, due to the increasingly deteriorating situation, although it has been reorganized repeatedly, it has still been opened and closed from time to time, and it is difficult to reverse the declining fortune. It is heard that the deficit in the past year has reached 500,000 yuan. After struggling to maintain it until the previous month, it was really unable to handle the aftermath, and finally stopped work and announced its closure. The total debt reached three million yuan. In addition to the deposited cotton yarn mortgage, which can be worth 1.45 million yuan, the actual loss is still 1.3 million yuan, which far exceeds the total capital. Last month, a shareholders' meeting was held in Shanghai, and all believed that a thorough liquidation was necessary. In addition to entrusting accountant Pan Xulun to be responsible for the liquidation, five people with the most shares were designated to be responsible for supervision. All accounts have now been sent to Shanghai, and the factory has also sent people to take care of them. Once the liquidation is completed, we will plan the method of closing. The largest creditor is the Industrial Bank, with more than 700,000 yuan, and Jiyuan Silver Company, with 450,000 yuan. It is predicted that priority creditors may be able to share some of them, but as for ordinary creditors, they are afraid that there will be no hope. From now on, the only industrial factory in Anhui Province has gone bankrupt and cannot survive. The livelihoods of thousands of people directly and indirectly will also be greatly panicked.

Chaoshan rice and plum food were originally extremely scarce, and all relied on foreign rice to provide relief. After the government levied foreign rice tax, the people's burden became heavier. At this time of rural economic bankruptcy, the people are poor and the wealth is exhausted, bearing this heavy burden, it is bound to be overturned. The Taiwanese smugglers, relying on special forces, openly took the opportunity to smuggle foreign rice into the country, resisting the payment of all taxes and donations. Tax and donation inspectors, because of fear of their fierce, do not dare to ask, let them transport in constantly. According to the investigation, from April 15 of this year to the present, the Taiwanese have transported a total of more than 50,000 bags of smuggled foreign rice, worth more than 400,000 yuan. This foreign rice avoids foreign rice tax of more than 200,000 yuan. After the sugar was implemented by selling the unified sale, the province-owned sugar sold only one product, and the foreign sugar was sold out.
